After checking the one the user thinks is correct, there is a Click to Check button at the end of each test which shows the scores the user got and the whole corrected test so that the user can easily see and find where he/she went wrong.\r\nDeclaration of data protection:\r\nThe app does not store or send any data of the users because they do not have to register in order to be able to use the app. However, the user can come into contact with me for help either through my web site or my email address I provided.
